  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_51a8d789-cc4a-4e31-957f-20bca9db30b8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

<span id="freeTextContainer9698443115540685874">I'm writing this because you begged. You know how I love the begging. In fact, you probably know too many things and know them far too well. Who am I?   <span id="freeText9698443115540685874" style="display:none">I'm writing this because you begged. You know how I love the begging. In fact, you probably know too many things and know them far too well. Who am I? Well, that's what I'm trying to figure out. I was a whore in my youth, a killer since my adolescence, and a monster as a man. I am the man who kidnapped Livvie. I am the man who held her in a dark room for weeks. But, most importantly, I am the man she loves. She loves me. It's quite sick, isn't it? Of course, there's more to our story than can be surmised in a few short sentences, but I'm at a loss for justifying my behavior back then. I assume if you're reading this, I don't need to make those justifications. You've already made your own. You're reading this because you want to know about the rest of the story. You want to know what happened that warm summer night in September of 2010, the night I met Livvie at The Paseo. It was the night my life changed all over again. It didn't happen exactly as Livvie said. She's been very kind to me in the retelling of our story. The truth is far more...complicated.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9698443115540685874" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">This book is Caleb's POV about what happen after they meet in Barcelona. The story is about their life together in Barcelona with some flashbacks. It <a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">This book is Caleb's POV about what happen after they meet in Barcelona. The story is about their life together in Barcelona with some flashbacks. It is completely different from the first 2 books.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer526122642" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11508525634897171416">6/18/13: <b> Alternate ending for Epilogue: The Dark Duet </b><br/>Watch video: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=gy0z5JXhAK4&feature=youtu.be'>http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=gy0z5J...</a><br/><br/>Read the alternate ending: <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ <br/><br/><b>EPILOGUE (ALTERNATE)</b><br/><br/>So, here we are at the end. Was it good for you? It was for me. I suppose in the end that’s all that really matters. I know that’s selfish, but you know I’m selfish and you love me anyway. <br/><br/>For what it’s worth, I think I might actually miss you.<br/><br/>Will you miss me? <br/><br/>Will you cry? <br/><br/>If you do, please drink a tear for me and know that I</span></span>
  <span id="freeText11508525634897171416" style="display:none">6/18/13: <b> Alternate ending for Epilogue: The Dark Duet </b><br />Watch video: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=gy0z5JXhAK4&amp;feature=youtu.be">http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=gy0z5J...</a><br /><br />Read the alternate ending: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ <br /><br /><b>EPILOGUE (ALTERNATE)</b><br /><br />So, here we are at the end. Was it good for you? It was for me. I suppose in the end that’s all that really matters. I know that’s selfish, but you know I’m selfish and you love me anyway. <br /><br />For what it’s worth, I think I might actually miss you.<br /><br />Will you miss me? <br /><br />Will you cry? <br /><br />If you do, please drink a tear for me and know that I never meant to cause you pain. Our parting is no cause to fret. In the words of Frank Herbert, “There is no real ending. It’s just the place where you stop the story.”<br /><br />Livvie and I go on. We still live and have adventures.<br /><br />Will we see each other again? I don’t have the answer to that. Life has caught me to expect the unexpected and it’s a lesson I learn over and again. Suffice to say – I hope so.<br /><br />To be perfectly honest, I’ve gone around and around trying to find the perfect ending to this novel I never intended to write. In the end, I’ve come to the conclusion that there wasn’t anything wrong with the way Livvie ended things. Her epilogue was short, but it captured the essence of our story: Survival is the most important thing. It affords us the chance to live and to find all of the things that make living worthwhile. I found redemption. I found forgiveness. I found love.<br /><br />That said, Livvie did a beautiful job with the ending and I can think of no greater tribute than to end this book as she wrote it (with my helpful commentary along the way of course). Submitted for your heartbreak, I present: The Epilogue (2.0)<br /><br />James swallowed thickly as he stared at the words on the screen. Sophia had written a very tragic love story, but it was a love story just the same. She had been very generous to him, painting a far better picture of the man he had been than he would have. <b>(I think we’ve learned this is absolutely true.)</b> She’d been working for weeks, sequestered in her little room upstairs. He wasn’t allowed in there, and though he didn’t like it, he respected Sophia’s wishes. He respected all her wishes these days. <b>(Because I’m the best boyfriend ever! Sorry, Rubio.)</b><br /><br />Several hours ago, she’d flown into the kitchen and thrown her arms around him.<br /><br />“Why are you smiling, Kitten? Did you finally finish?” James asked.<br /><br />“Yes! I finished,” she said and followed up with a little dance. <b>(I love the little dance.)</b> She’d immediately dragged him upstairs and planted him in front of the laptop so he could start reading. There wasn’t another chair, so she’d gotten down on her knees and rested her head on his knee. <b>(She lies; she just likes kneeling at my feet.)</b><br /><br />As he read, he stroked her hair. James had been scared to read everything from Sophia’s point of view, but he was glad he’d made it through and discovered just how Sophia remembered everything. She loved him, he was sure of it, and while he still didn’t think he deserved it, he was happy about it nonetheless. <b>(This is entirely true.)</b><br /><br />He once again gazed on her sleeping form, unable to resist shifting her hair away from her face and behind her ear. Her mouth was slack, and he was sure she had drooled on him, but it didn’t matter. She was the most beautiful thing he had ever seen. He couldn’t help but stroke her. He loved the soft noises she made when he did. He didn’t deserve her. He never did <b>(also true)</b>.<br /><br />She’d been with him for over a year now, and secretly he always hoped she would tire of him and decide to leave. <b>(I didn’t hope—I feared.)</b> She told him she loved him often, <b>(I’ll give this to her. She did tell me she loved me often—not with her words, but with her deeds)</b> and each time, it cut him down to his core. He didn’t deserve her love <b>(no, I don’t)</b>. He couldn’t bring himself to pretend he did <b>(no, I can’t)</b>.<br /> <br />When he’d learned she’d been writing their story, he helped her in any way he could. It was his outlet as much as hers. He needed to see it in black and white – the pain he put her through, the monster he had been. He never wanted to forget what he could never allow himself to become again <b>(true)</b>.<br /> <br />Since the night Sophia had met him at the Paseo, the night he had decided to leave everything behind and integrate into mainstream society, so much of him had changed. Away from the horrors of his youth, away from blood and vengeance, he was just – James.<br /><br />At first, he’d had no idea what to do with himself. All around him, real life was happening, and he was a spectator. What did he know about meeting people in cafés? About having friends that weren’t killers? <b>(I love you, Livvie.)</b><br /><br />But at night, in the dark, when he found he couldn’t sleep because the world felt suddenly too big – there was Sophia <b>(yes)</b>.<br /><br />Whenever he thought about running away and returning to the life he knew, he thought about the day he’d given her the note. She’d burst into tears and run away from the café. He’d thought she would call the FBI, and he’d been prepared to go to prison if they were the ones to meet him at the Paseo. <b>(It sounds silly… now.)</b><br /><br />Instead, she had met him there. She stood, looking like a goddess among commoners. Her hair lay in soft waves down her back, occasionally being picked up by the breeze. She wore a black halter dress that hugged her breasts and bared her back. She also wore incredibly tall heels. They were dangerous, considering the cobbled streets. She’d wanted him to know she was a grown woman, and she wasn’t afraid of him anymore. <b>(I can still picture this in my mind.)</b><br /><br />He approached her from across the square. He was nervous. He wore jeans and a black cashmere sweater. The sleeves were pushed up to his forearms. He wanted her to know he was different. He didn’t want to hurt her anymore.<br /><br />Her back was to him as he approached, but the breeze suddenly died and she turned when she heard his steps approaching.<br /><br />There had been no words. He simply stood in front of her with his hands in his pockets. Her breath caught, and for a while she only stared at him. She stepped closer, and he almost took a step back – but didn’t. She was suddenly very close, and he couldn’t help but inhale her scent and close his eyes. <b>(I love the way she smells.)</b> She touched his shirt and pulled him down. His head swam. <b>(It did!)</b> Then she kissed him, and it was all that needed to be said.<br /><br />He moved to Barcelona so she could still attend university. They never talked about the past. When people asked them how they met, she was quick to intercept the question and respond. They had met at the Paseo de Colon. <b>(If only it had been so simple.)</b><br /> <br />When they made love, he was surprised to discover Sophia’s tastes had evolved. She wanted him to spank her. She wanted him to bind her arms. He felt sick about it at first. Her proclivities were obviously his fault. Still, their games turned him on to the point of physical pain. <b>(They still do.)</b><br /><br />He felt villainous, but what was done was done, and now he would do everything he could to give her what she wanted. He owed her much. Besides, it wasn’t always rough. Sometimes it was vanilla – and he liked that too <b>(very much)</b>.<br /><br />Carefully, James lifted Sophia into his arms and carried her to their bedroom. He laid her down on the bed, smiling as she shifted around, seeking some way to get comfortable. He undressed and got in bed next to her. Just touching her made him hard. He owed her so much. <b>(Only everything.)</b><br /><br />Suddenly overwhelmed, he held her impossibly tight. She whimpered and whined until her eyes opened and she stared up at his face. “Oh my god, what’s wrong?” she asked and stroked his distressed face. <br /><br />“I love you,” he whispered. <br /><br />“I love you, too,” she replied. Sophia’s eyes welled up with tears and she tilted her face toward his. <br /><br />She kissed him so passionately, so sweetly, that James thought if she never kissed him again, this was the kiss he always wanted to remember <b>(it still is)</b>.<br /><br />I could never write an ending better than the one Livvie gave you, but I’ll leave you with this: Once upon a time I saved Livvie. She’s been saving me ever since.<br /><br /><b> The End </b><br /> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />6/12/13: I have started traveling for book signings so I'm hit/miss on communication. <div id="review_525503992" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/525503992" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/525503992?book_show_action=true">Feb 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer525503992" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16221154540380887524"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408002i/797661._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> ****** VERY IMPORTANT MESSAGE ******</b><br/><br/><b> For those of you who pre-ordered and are getting your copies downloaded now, the WRONG VERSION of the book was sent out!!! <br/><br/>If your version does not have 15 Chapters + an epilogue, PLEASE DO NOT READ IT and a corrected version will be out soon!! </b><br/><br/>***************************<br/><br/>WOW!!! (<u> FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED </u> )<br/><br/>A few months ago, very late one night, C.J. Roberts released the beginning of an epilogue to THE DARK DUET and I utterly blown away by how amazing it was. N</span>
  <span id="freeText16221154540380887524" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408002i/797661._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> ****** VERY IMPORTANT MESSAGE ******</b><br><br><b> For those of you who pre-ordered and are getting your copies downloaded now, the WRONG VERSION of the book was sent out!!! <br><br>If your version does not have 15 Chapters + an epilogue, PLEASE DO NOT READ IT and a corrected version will be out soon!! </b><br><br>***************************<br><br>WOW!!! (<u> FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED </u> )<br><br>A few months ago, very late one night, C.J. Roberts released the beginning of an epilogue to THE DARK DUET and I utterly blown away by how amazing it was. Not long after she announced that it would be turned into a full-length epilogue book. This is that book.<br><br><u> <b> WARNING </b> </u><br><br><b>✦ IF YOU HAVE NOT READ THE DARK DUET, DO NOT READ THIS REVIEW!! </b><br><br>Instead, go to book #1,<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12513614.Captive_in_the_Dark__The_Dark_Duet___1_" title="Captive in the Dark (The Dark Duet, #1) by C.J. Roberts" rel="nofollow noopener">Captive in the Dark</a>, and start there.<br><br><b> ✦ If you have read the first 2 books though, then this is a <u>spoiler-free</u> review.</b><br><br>The Dark Duet series is one of my all-time favorite stories and so when I found out that there was going to be an epilogue my heart literally just stopped for a moment!! I couldn’t even read it right away because even just the possibility of it brought back a whole slew of strong, heart-clenching emotions I had wrapped up after having finished the series.<br><br>My heart was pounding <b> pounding </b> POUNDING. Every detail of the story and my connection to the characters came flooding back to me. From the very first line I was just propelled *right* back to the exact moment that the story had left off. I was right there. My whole heart was involved, instantly. I was *with* it every word of the way. I’m not kidding – it was perfect! <br><br>In this epilogue we get to see the story from Caleb’s POV. It takes us back to that scene at the end of book #2 and moved forward from there but this time showing us the story through his eyes…<br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> “I missed you every day, Kitten. Every. Fucking. Day.” </b></i>
</blockquote>  <br>I loved that it felt exactly like Caleb was talking right to me. Ok, us. Ok, the readers. But I can pretend it was me. I felt like it was me. My world just shut down and it was just me hanging onto every detail of the story he told.<br><br>The tables were turned in this book and we got to see his frustrations at being in the position of needing HER acceptance. He always had been dominant by nature and so it was a true sign of his love for her that he kept trying to hold himself back and give HER exactly what she needed from him.<br><br>“I had gone through all sorts of scenarios in my head prior to making contact with Livvie. However, her passive aggressive behavior toward me was not one of them. My mind is much more problem/solution oriented. Mad at me? Scream at me. Punch me if you’re up to it. Please don’t smile at me sweetly, act like nothing is wrong and then leave me disillusioned. And before you say anything, yes — I realize how fucking ironic my words are. I have played my fair share on mind games with Livvie. It doesn’t mean I liked being on the other side. No man does.”  <br><br>He tried to play nice and, he was a good person at heart (we all know this) but the truth of it is that he is not nice. He’s not your white picket fence. He’s your dark-and-twisted. But he’s also the guy who loved her with his whole heart and it just broke my mine to see him trying SO hard.<br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> “I know you deserve to be happy. I know you deserve someone… better, but I’m selfish. I want you. I want you bad enough to try and be someone better.” </b></i>
</blockquote>  <br>I loved watching them rediscover each other. They had one hell of a history together but this was like starting fresh to a certain extent – removed from the nightmare, and in a new environment with new hopes and new possibilities.<br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> “No, Kitten. I’m not okay,” I whispered. “I don’t know how long it’s going to take for me to be okay. I just know that as long as you’re with me, there’s a chance that one day… I might be.” </b></i>
</blockquote>  <br>I loved that this truly was an Epilogue in every sense of the word. To me, an epilogue is the happily ever after and with Caleb and Livvie, it wasn’t just a question of slipping into one as so many other book couples do because after the intensly dark and emotional journey of the first two books, it was believable that they would have to work hard to find the exact balance of happy that worked for them. This Epilogue wasn’t just another book in the series, but rather a detailed and focused continuation of how they rebuilt their lives and their relationship.<br><br>It’s not often (okay, it’s not ever) that we get to see something like this – an epilogue turned into an entire book. We’ve been through the nightmares and the pain of their journey through the dark but now it was time for them both to find a way to live in the light.<br><br>I loved that there was no external drama in this book – it was all focused on the main characters. It literally just showed the struggles of two people try to move on from what they’d been through. It showed the emotional conflict, the questions, the uncertainties, the desires, and most strongly the knowledge that they both needed each other more than anything else in the world. They’d been through so much together and just had to find the way to live with that.<br><br>The truth of it is that what happened to Livvie was not okay. What happened to Caleb was not okay. But just because bad things happen, it doesn’t mean there can be no moving forward.<br><br><blockquote> <i> “I didn’t want to hurt her. I loved her. I didn’t know how to do it like normal people. I didn’t know how to tell her how scared I was.” </i>
</blockquote>  <br>Their happily-ever-after wasn’t fairy tale perfect but at the same time, I absolutely loved the message it conveyed that even people with the most utterly fucked up pasts could still find their slice of happiness – however unconventional it might be. The point is that they found what worked for them. And that was just absolutely beautiful.<br><br><blockquote> <i> “I know it’s odd between us. How could it not be? We don’t know each other in this world, but I’ve seen you at your worst, and what I know is that you’d do anything to protect me. That’s enough for now. The rest will come.” </i>
</blockquote>  <br>I think that this story was so important to tell because after the events that they lived through in the first two books, in order to fully connect with and understand what made them able to move on to their future while living with their pasts, the explanation was necessary to fully show the readers more than just their love for each other but the literally process of how they came to their decisions.<br><br>I truly feel that Caleb and Livvie’s story has now come full circle. There are few stories out there that take the time to actually give the readers such a complete picture of the ‘happily ever after’ and it’s a rare and special thing for the readers to experience especially considering the strong levels of emotional connection that bonded us to the characters in the first two books.<br><br>The journey they have been through is one of a kind. Twisted. Fucked up. Scarring. Beautiful.<br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> “I had come to understand our relationship would be riddled with moments where the past sucked all the joy out of the present. My only hope was that with enough time, Livvie and I would build memories capable of trumping our beginning.” </b></i>
</blockquote>  <br><br><u> RELEASE DATE: June 15, 2013.</u><br><br>If you haven’t read this series yet, I strongly urge you to give it a shot. It is truly in a category on its own. It will test you. Test you to the very possible limit. But oh-my-GOD is it EVER worth it!!<br><br>This entire series has a beautiful but utterly RAW and honest intensity to it. It just pulls at your heart. You can’t help but be drawn in. C.J. Roberts’ writing is addictive. Its compelling, beautiful, and deeply evocative. She is honestly one of the most talented authors I’ve read.<br><br>I won’t lie though, this story is NOT for the faint of heart. It is captivating, yet deeply twisted… very disturbing and yet truly beautiful. It is gritty and powerful. But honestly, if you feel brave enough to give it a go, its one of *those* stories that you won’t forget.<br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> “I’d kill for you, Livvie. I’d die for you.” </b></i>
</blockquote>  <br><br><b> Series rating: 5 ++ stars! </b><br><br><br>Here’s the reading order:<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12513614.Captive_in_the_Dark__The_Dark_Duet___1_" title="Captive in the Dark (The Dark Duet, #1) by C.J. Roberts" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1315343569s/12513614.jpg" alt="Captive in the Dark (The Dark Duet, #1) by C.J. Roberts" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13612739.Seduced_in_the_Dark__The_Dark_Duet___2_" title="Seduced in the Dark (The Dark Duet, #2) by C.J. Roberts" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1335114363s/13612739.jpg" alt="Seduced in the Dark (The Dark Duet, #2) by C.J. Roberts" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17317675.Epilogue__The_Dark_Duet___3_" title="Epilogue (The Dark Duet, #3) by C.J. Roberts" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1360713467s/17317675.jpg" alt="Epilogue (The Dark Duet, #3) by C.J. Roberts" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>My casting: <br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380364858i/716648._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380391196i/753388.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380364858i/716649._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>BLURB --&gt; <i> I’m writing this because you begged. You know how I love the begging. In fact, you probably know too many things and know them far too well.<br><br>Who am I?<br><br>Well, that’s what I’m trying to figure out. I was a whore in my youth, a killer since my adolescence, and a monster as a man. I am the man who kidnapped Livvie. I am the man who held her in a dark room for weeks. But, most importantly, I am the man she loves.<br><br>She loves me. It’s quite sick, isn’t it?<br><br>Of course, there’s more to our story than can be surmised in a few short sentences, but I’m at a loss for justifying my behavior back then. I assume if you’re reading this, I don’t need to make those justifications. You’ve already made your own.<br><br>You’re reading this because you want to know about the rest of the story. You want to know what happened that warm summer night in September of 2010, the night I met Livvie at The Paseo. It was the night my life changed all over again.<br><br>It didn’t happen exactly as Livvie said. She’s been very kind to me in the retelling of our story. The truth is far more…complicated. </i><br><br><b>For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="16221154540380887524" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_526294857" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/526294857" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/526294857?book_show_action=true">Feb 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=2013-release">2013-release</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=favorite-series">favorite-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=male-pov">male-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=unputdownable">unputdownable</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=hot-hot-hot">hot-hot-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=swoonworthy-male-lead">swoonworthy-male-lead</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer526294857" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4879998430774730368"><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Livvie, I'll forgive you whatever the hell you want. You don't need my forgiveness; you never have to ask for it. It's yours, Livvie. Anything that's mine to give is already yours."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408124i/798170.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>PERFECT EPILOGUE TO AN ALREADY PERFECT SERIES.</b> <br/><br/>The Dark Duet series is one of the most messed up, dark, twisted, excrutiating, emotional series I've ever read. It's also one of the BEST series I've ever read. So, when I heard there was going to be an epilogue, I <i>knew</i> it was going to be <b>EPIC</b>. And well, tha</span>
  <span id="freeText4879998430774730368" style="display:none"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Livvie, I'll forgive you whatever the hell you want. You don't need my forgiveness; you never have to ask for it. It's yours, Livvie. Anything that's mine to give is already yours."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408124i/798170.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>PERFECT EPILOGUE TO AN ALREADY PERFECT SERIES.</b> <br><br>The Dark Duet series is one of the most messed up, dark, twisted, excrutiating, emotional series I've ever read. It's also one of the BEST series I've ever read. So, when I heard there was going to be an epilogue, I <i>knew</i> it was going to be <b>EPIC</b>. And well, that's exactly what it was, to me at least. I loved every single second of this beautiful and unforgettable story and wanted to highlight almost every single sentence. And reading it from Caleb' POV for a change, made it al the more memorable.<br><br>~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~<br><br><b>Livvie --</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408002i/797665._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Caleb --</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408124i/798171._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"While I no longer kill, I am a killer. A killer in love is a very dangerously thing."</b><br><br>Caleb has come a long way from the person he used to be when he and Livvie first met. He's no longer the coldhearted person he used to be, but he's not exactly Prince Charming yet either. He still has his flaws but that's exactly what made me love him so much. He's not perfect, far from it actually, but for Livvie, he's willing to fight and try to the be the best possible version of himself.<br><br><b>"I missed you every day, Kitten. Every. Fucking. Day."</b><br><br>At the same time, Livvie has to fight some of her own demons. She knows she loves Caleb, but sometimes the past still resurfaces and it's hard for her to relive those memories. But, Livvie is now a much stronger person than she used to be. She stands her own ground and she doesn't give in whenever she and Caleb have an argument. Finally, they can be themselves around each other and be honest about their true feelings, although it's still hard for them to express what they're truly feeling.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408124i/798172.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>***<br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I am the man who kidnapped Livvie. I am the man who held her in a dark room for weeks. I'm the one who tied her to a bedpost and beat her. I'm the one who nearly sold her into sexual slavery. But, most importantly, I am the man she loves. <br>She loves me. It's quite sick, isn't it?"</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408124i/798173._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Trying to lead a normal life after everything they've been through isn't easy for either of them but together they try to make the best of it. Together with Livvie's new friends, Claudia and Rubio, they try to build up a everyday life for themselves, filled with love, laughter and celebrations but also filled with some painful trips down memory lane. Still, I can't count the many moments I've literally laughed out loud with one of Caleb's hilariously honest inner monologues or the playful banter between him and Livvie, that showed, once again, how perfect they are for each other.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"We're pretty far from perfect, Kitten. I'm the most fucked up person you know."<br><br>"Yeah, but I'm the second most fucked up person I know, and when you put two negatives together, you get a positive. That's math, Caleb. Math is the language of the universe. You can't argue with the universe." <br>Her grin was patently ridiculous. I love you so damn much.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408124i/798174.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"There was only one thing the void wanted. Greedily tearing me apart, it asked for Livvie. It asked for my hopes, my dreams. It wanted my memories of her face. It wanted the laughter we had shared. "Mine," the void had decreed. Only Livvie could make me whole, and as soon as I realized it, I couldn't stop looking for her."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>The way the story ends, suggests that it might not be the end of the series after all... And I can only hope that that really sinter case and that there's even more Caleb and Livvie to come! But even if it's not, I'm happy with the way things ended and no matter what, Caleb and Livvie will forever continue to live on in our hearts and minds.<br><br><b>"There is no real ending. It's just the place where you stop the story."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408124i/798175._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b><i>"No, Kitten. I'm not okay," I whispered. "I don't know how long it's going to take for me to be okay. I just know that as long as you're with me, there's a chance that one day...I might be."</i><br><br>♥♥♥</b>
</blockquote><br></span>

<div id="review_525434292" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/525434292" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/525434292?book_show_action=true">Feb 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer525434292" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer243083858860293402"><b>5 Stars!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/9e3cbd6e-54a9-46fb-8101-e9e49f49b443_zps185f8f60.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407991i/797561.jpg' alt=' photo 9e3cbd6e-54a9-46fb-8101-e9e49f49b443_zps185f8f60.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>
  <blockquote>I’m writing this because you begged. You know how I love the begging.</blockquote>
</b><br/>It’s been a year. A year since everything changed. A year to find Livvie. A year to find himself. <br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/0abf65ba-3925-44ba-bfe5-fc8ea77033d7_zps5c99125c.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407991i/797562.jpg' alt=' photo 0abf65ba-3925-44ba-bfe5-fc8ea77033d7_zps5c99125c.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>
  <i>“I missed you every day, Kitten. Every. Fucking. Day.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>This is an extended epilogue of the Dark Duet, told completley from Caleb’s pov. Yes- you heard that right! A whole book from Caleb. Caleb is the best narrator. It feels like he is sitting right by you, telling you his story. I loved every word of this! <br/><br/>I</span>
  <span id="freeText243083858860293402" style="display:none"><b>5 Stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/9e3cbd6e-54a9-46fb-8101-e9e49f49b443_zps185f8f60.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407991i/797561.jpg" alt=" photo 9e3cbd6e-54a9-46fb-8101-e9e49f49b443_zps185f8f60.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>I’m writing this because you begged. You know how I love the begging.</blockquote>
</b><br>It’s been a year. A year since everything changed. A year to find Livvie. A year to find himself. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/0abf65ba-3925-44ba-bfe5-fc8ea77033d7_zps5c99125c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407991i/797562.jpg" alt=" photo 0abf65ba-3925-44ba-bfe5-fc8ea77033d7_zps5c99125c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>“I missed you every day, Kitten. Every. Fucking. Day.”</i>
</b><br><br>This is an extended epilogue of the Dark Duet, told completley from Caleb’s pov. Yes- you heard that right! A whole book from Caleb. Caleb is the best narrator. It feels like he is sitting right by you, telling you his story. I loved every word of this! <br><br>It takes Caleb and Kitten some time to figure things out. They don’t immediately jump into their happy ever after. It takes time. Building back trust. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“You are the best thing that’s ever happened to me, Caleb. You’re also the worst. I’m trying to reconcile those two things.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Livvie is still trying to process everything that happened. She is trying to move on with her life. She has friends who care about her, she is going to school. Caleb showing up rattles everything. Caleb is trying to change. He wants to be different, but its a struggle. All he really knows is that he needs Livvie. It scares him how much he needs her, but he does. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/2105af2c-876f-4e61-8c62-ec893acf4ba2_zps1a37ccce.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407991i/797563.jpg" alt=" photo 2105af2c-876f-4e61-8c62-ec893acf4ba2_zps1a37ccce.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Caleb is still himself, but you get to see a different side of him as well. I love both. I just love all things Caleb! He and Livvie are not perfect people. They both may be a little screwed up, but they are perfect for each other. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/111c5026-9e94-455e-a21a-2f0f09615e18_zpsdf8842aa.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407991i/797564.jpg" alt=" photo 111c5026-9e94-455e-a21a-2f0f09615e18_zpsdf8842aa.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And it is HOT, and KINKY, and VERY VERY SEXY! Let me just say that Caleb does not disappoint ;)<br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/ffddb578-2b3e-4dde-8024-134a612f1ede_zpsb99ac169.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407991i/797565.jpg" alt=" photo ffddb578-2b3e-4dde-8024-134a612f1ede_zpsb99ac169.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This story was entertaining, captivating, and a must read for all readers of ‘The Dark Duet.’ If you haven’t read The Dark Duet, you are really missing out. Caleb is rough around the edges, but he is charming, funny, intriguing, and sexy as hell! It was wonderful to see Caleb and Livvie’s journey after everything. Epilogue is Caleb’s story- completely from his pov, it shows his innermost thoughts, his feelings, and his growth. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/44fe6098-5c88-443b-8884-383ee34aa5fb_zps11f90591.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407991i/797566.jpg" alt=" photo 44fe6098-5c88-443b-8884-383ee34aa5fb_zps11f90591.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>CJ Roberts is an amazingly talented author. One of my favorite ‘dark reads’ and I look forward to many more books by her! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/e7c8c47a-8e7e-478e-95bd-43f1caa01e57_zps0196f7b2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407991i/797567.jpg" alt=" photo e7c8c47a-8e7e-478e-95bd-43f1caa01e57_zps0196f7b2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/525423246" />
    <a title="Alexis *Reality Bites*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5587514-alexis-reality-bites"><img alt="Alexis *Reality Bites*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1404308282p2/5587514.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/525423246?book_show_action=true">Feb 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alexis *Reality Bites*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alexis *Reality Bites*" href="/user/show/5587514-alexis-reality-bites">Alexis *Reality Bites*</a>
      </span>

        rated it

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer525423246" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16396971989940211071"><b>QUICK REVIEW/Minor Spoilers</b> -mature content reader discretion is advised.<br/>4.5 STARS out of 5<br/>Genre: Adult Romance -Erotica(Do not read if you have not read books#1 and #2 in this series)<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407989ra/797555.gif' alt=' photo happy1.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407989ra/797556.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_inline_mm5isksl0N1rbnfwj_zps53af28d2.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>Quick read but a goodread! The captor of our hearts Caleb, takes us on a journey of how he and Livvie learn to move forward after going through hell and back. Caleb finds himself asking "Who am I" at the age of 27, an age when most have figured such a thing out. Yet in a sense he is just beginning.<br/><br/>If you have read </span>
  <span id="freeText16396971989940211071" style="display:none"><b>QUICK REVIEW/Minor Spoilers</b> -mature content reader discretion is advised.<br>4.5 STARS out of 5<br>Genre: Adult Romance -Erotica(Do not read if you have not read books#1 and #2 in this series)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407989ra/797555.gif" alt=" photo happy1.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407989ra/797556.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_inline_mm5isksl0N1rbnfwj_zps53af28d2.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Quick read but a goodread! The captor of our hearts Caleb, takes us on a journey of how he and Livvie learn to move forward after going through hell and back. Caleb finds himself asking "Who am I" at the age of 27, an age when most have figured such a thing out. Yet in a sense he is just beginning.<br><br>If you have read The Dark Duet series then you are familiar with his back story as a child prostitute, as a killer, as an abductor. You are painfully aware that this is not easy for him to move on from that life to live a normal one... A life with out<br> <b>killing <br> abducting <br> and training women to be sex slaves.</b> <br>On top of that the woman he loves was once his captive. And she is still trying to move on from the traumatic experience that forever changed her life.<br><br> So now here he stands wanting her, loving her and hoping in his heart that she returns his sentiments. And she does in equal measure. But the pain is still raw and she let's him know it.<br><br><br><i>“Did you realize you loved me while I was alone in the hospital and weeping over you? When did you shout your love from the rooftops, Caleb? I couldn’t hear you. I was too busy trying to fucking breathe without you. I was busy convincing everyone around me I wasn’t crazy for defending my kidnapper. So, remind me. When did you say the words? I’ll be sure to go back in time and comfort the broken girl you left in your wake. Your love can comfort her, because I’m not the same person anymore..."</i> ~Livvie<br><br>At times this book was a hard pill to swallow. Two emotionally damaged people the inflicter and his tormented prisoner what a pair. Some how they make it work he comes to accept the new Livvie, her new life and her new friends. However in between the emotionally charged fights and the incredibly delicious sex scenes I feel like the book ended and Caleb is still trying to find himself now as James. Or maybe a better way to say it is, he is accepting himself as James. I don't know.<br> I did not feel....closure. <br>Am I alone on this???<br><br>On top of that the ending had a "for now" sign on it. THE END(for now) Is it possible we'll hear from these two again? I hope so!<br><br><br><b> C A P T I V E</b><br><i>This is not a romance. Romances are filled with valiant men and simpering damsels in distress. Romances have heroes worthy of the title. They slay dragons and climb towers to rescue beautiful princesses they immediately marry and impregnate. Romances end with a happily ever after. This is not a romance. This is a love story. The characters are flawed to the point of being broken. The hero is beautiful, but ugly in ways that defy the ordinary imagination. The heroine isn’t trapped in a tower, but a dark and lonely room. There is no prince coming to save her. While love blooms and thrives, there is no happily ever after. Love does not always begin or end the way we wish it would.<b> A love story can happen to anyone. This one happened to me.</b></i> ~Livvie<br> <br><br><u>
  <b>Fave Lines</b>
</u><br><br><i>“I’m writing this because you begged. You know how I love the begging”</i> -Caleb<br><br><i>“Everything is in the process of becoming something else. It’s the law of change.”</i> -Caleb<br><br><i>“I've seen you handle your stick, Caleb. You're much better at it than I am”</i> -Livvie<br><br><i>“You be rational, Caleb. You show up out of the fucking blue and just expect me to fall on my back and throw my legs open for you? No! Not until I know what the hell you’ve been up to for the last year. Not until I know why you’re back in my life and what you expect from me.”</i> -Livvie<br><br><i>“Misery I understand. Happiness is terrifying."</i> -Caleb<br><br><i>“What does a former kidnapper/murderer do in retirement?"</i> -Caleb<br><br><br>My Ratings<br>Characters- Strong Willed and Lovable<br>Writing Style- Excellent! My preferred cup of tea!<br>Plot/Storyline- Solid<br>Steam Factor- High/Very Steamy<br>Overall- I LOVED IT!!!!!! A MUST READ!!!<br><b><br>Now go forth and read. Then come tell us about it on Goodreads!</b><br>For more reviews got to <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogspot.com">http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogs...</a><br><br></span>

<div id="review_525418465" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Rosalinda *KRASNORADA*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12788865-rosalinda-krasnorada"><img alt="Rosalinda *KRASNORADA*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1583582487p2/12788865.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/525418465?book_show_action=true">Feb 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rosalinda *KRASNORADA*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rosalinda *KRASNORADA*" href="/user/show/12788865-rosalinda-krasnorada">Rosalinda *KRASNORADA*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Rosalinda *KRASNORADA* by: </span>
      Soraya Naomi
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer525418465" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12479903526104806435"><br/><b> <blockquote>Love does not always begin or end the way we wish it would.<br/> A love story can happen to anyone. This one happened to me </blockquote> </b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407988i/797540.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I can’t even remember the number of times I’ve said The Dark Duet is one of my all time fave series and I’ll keep recommending this series to everyone but in all fairness, this book was not as good as Seduced in the Dark. Then I have to give credit to C.J. because she had a difficult job to do.<br/><br/><b>***PLEASE DO NOT READ THIS REVIEW IF YOU HAVEN’T READ THIS SERIES***</b><br/><br/>I’ve read all th</span>
  <span id="freeText12479903526104806435" style="display:none"><br><b> <blockquote>Love does not always begin or end the way we wish it would.<br> A love story can happen to anyone. This one happened to me </blockquote> </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407988i/797540.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I can’t even remember the number of times I’ve said The Dark Duet is one of my all time fave series and I’ll keep recommending this series to everyone but in all fairness, this book was not as good as Seduced in the Dark. Then I have to give credit to C.J. because she had a difficult job to do.<br><br><b>***PLEASE DO NOT READ THIS REVIEW IF YOU HAVEN’T READ THIS SERIES***</b><br><br>I’ve read all the reviews from my buddies and they did a kick ass job so let’s keep this short and nice.<br><br>The first 40/45% of Epilogue was clearly a 5 stars book for me. I wanted to know what happened when Caleb &amp; Livvie saw each other at the Paseo and I liked the way Livvie handled things. She was not an innocent girl anymore, not after what she has been through. Then, things sweetened up a little bit and I was kind of bored for moments.<br><br>I don’t want you guys to take this wrong, C.J. writing style is still music to my ears but the story was not what I was expecting in the second half of the book. I guess I wanted an Epilogue but this was more of a sequel for me and I have issues with sequels after HEAs but this is MY ISSUE so it’s me the one with the problem. The book is totally fine, just not for me.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote> Someone once told me you shouldn’t let vendettas run your life </blockquote>
</b><br><br>The book starts right after Livvie meets Caleb at the Paseo. I was a crying mess when reading that at the end of SITD and I was really looking forward to that moment again when I started Epilogue. It didn’t disappoint, it was great and real. I mean, we cannot expect Livvie to do not ask questions or to trust him no matter what. I like real things, I like real heroines and I loved that part.<br><br>But then as the story goes on and things start to ‘settle’ between them I am not sure this is Caleb we are talking about. I mean, MY Caleb from The Dark Duet. And I know he’s obviously changed and all but he was sooooo cheesy sometimes. I don’t like cheesy Caleb.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote> Happiness is terrifying </blockquote>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407988i/797541._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So overall I enjoyed some parts but I didn’t enjoyed another parts. I am happy I read this one anyway because as I said, I loved the first half of the book and also that part around 60% when <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ they speak about her book, that was very emotional  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br><br>This being said, I will be reading <b>Agent Reed </b> book, I actually can’t wait for it. I know C.J. can deliver what we are expecting. This is how I am picturing him right now.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407988i/797542._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> Ladies, you can spank me now for not giving this 5 stars, can't wait! You all know how much I love a good spanking...</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_534441071" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/534441071" />
    <a title="Jamie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11971939-jamie"><img alt="Jamie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1450934094p2/11971939.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/534441071?book_show_action=true">Feb 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jamie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jamie" href="/user/show/11971939-jamie">Jamie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer534441071" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4019293564471127266"><i>
  <b>♥♥♥ FANFUCKINGTASTIC!!!♥♥♥</b>
</i><br/> <br/><br/>One of my all time favorite series comes to a close and it could not have gone out better than this. Epilogue lived up to every one of my expectations. <br/><br/>Epilogue starts off with Caleb deciding to give us his side of the story.. what happened after we left off in The Dark Duet.<br/><br/><i>
  <b>I’m writing this because you begged. You know how I love the begging. In fact, you probably know too many things and know them far too well.</b>
</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409391i/801594._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Caleb tells us his story of his journey to win Li</span>
  <span id="freeText4019293564471127266" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>♥♥♥ FANFUCKINGTASTIC!!!♥♥♥</b>
</i><br> <br><br>One of my all time favorite series comes to a close and it could not have gone out better than this. Epilogue lived up to every one of my expectations. <br><br>Epilogue starts off with Caleb deciding to give us his side of the story.. what happened after we left off in The Dark Duet.<br><br><i>
  <b>I’m writing this because you begged. You know how I love the begging. In fact, you probably know too many things and know them far too well.</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409391i/801594._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Caleb tells us his story of his journey to win Livvie back. Although she is still deeply and irrevocably in love with Caleb, he still has to prove that he's not going anywhere....that she means as much to him as he does to her. Caleb is completely obsessed with Livvie and will do whatever it takes to keep her.. the pain he felt while they were apart was just as great as hers.<br><br><i>
  <b>It wasn’t until Livvie walked away and I was truly alone in the world that I began to feel what love could be. It didn’t come to me as it came to others; I had to find love as I had found everything else that defined me: through my suffering. The chasm Livvie’s absence opened in me was a hungry void. It was alive, the void, and it would not be filled with vengeance. It was not soothed by my attempts to right my wrongs. It was not pleased by random women. It did not sleep, despite the amount of drink I imbibed to dull my senses.</b>
</i><br><br>One of the things I loved most about this book was that although Caleb had set out to reclaim Livvie, he was still his dark and twisty self with the sharp sexual edge we've come to love about him. Caleb still knows how to make Kitten's body react just the way he wants..and he's relentless....<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409391i/801595.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>We get to see Caleb grow...his love for Livvie so enormous that there is nothing he wouldn't do for her. He knows he doesn't deserve Livvie, but he wants to be a better man <i>
  <b>FOR</b>
</i> her. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409391i/801596._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yes, this was an amazing end to the story of Caleb and Livvie but I'm sad it's over. I can only hope that perhaps C.J. might give us a little something extra later on, a little taste of where they are in the future *crosses fingers*. <br><br>This is definitely a MUST READ series in my opinion..but it's not for the faint of heart. It's very dark and upsetting at times but it's a truly stunning story. Not many books have made me feel as confused about my feelings as C.J. was able to do with The Dark Duet series and I'm thankful for the journey she took me on. This is what a good book does, it takes you into the story and doesn't let you go. I've never read another character like Caleb and I'm quite sure I never will. He's one of a kind...<br><br><i>So, goodbye Caleb *sniffles* I hope your able to drop us a line and check in one day in the not to distant future; but until then.. I got nothing but love for you baby!!</i> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/376981.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="4019293564471127266" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_525418689" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="La-Lionne" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11644154-la-lionne"><img alt="La-Lionne" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1458815714p2/11644154.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/525418689?book_show_action=true">Feb 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="La-Lionne" class="user" itemprop="url" name="La-Lionne" href="/user/show/11644154-la-lionne">La-Lionne</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=action-packed">action-packed</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=brilliant-ending">brilliant-ending</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=hot">hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=mafia-gangs">mafia-gangs</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer525418689" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16967596897824270415"><u>
  <b>Added June 28th</b>
</u><br/><br/>Did I jus imagined that I read C. J. Roberts saying on FB that this hunk of a man is cast in TDD TV series? <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1435505770i/15354297._SY540_.jpg' width='280' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>------------------------------------------------------<br/><b>5 extraordinary stars!</b><br/><br/>Thank you for the ride C. J. Roberts, I enjoyed every single word of it.<br/>I can't believe the journey ends here :-(.<br/><br/>It was one helluva unforgettable ride. I think at this point analyses of the book is unnecessary. Those who've read C.J Roberts previous books know that she is brilliant at what she d</span>
  <span id="freeText16967596897824270415" style="display:none"><u>
  <b>Added June 28th</b>
</u><br><br>Did I jus imagined that I read C. J. Roberts saying on FB that this hunk of a man is cast in TDD TV series? <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1435505770i/15354297._SY540_.jpg" width="280" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>------------------------------------------------------<br><b>5 extraordinary stars!</b><br><br>Thank you for the ride C. J. Roberts, I enjoyed every single word of it.<br>I can't believe the journey ends here :-(.<br><br>It was one helluva unforgettable ride. I think at this point analyses of the book is unnecessary. Those who've read C.J Roberts previous books know that she is brilliant at what she does. You either got it or you don't, and she's GOT IT :-D. <br><br>All I can think about at this point is the fact that TDD series has come to an end. I feel like I should wait a day or two to write the review, but here comes my babble :).<br><br>This books isn't as intense as her previous books, but just as emotional. It's about Livvie and Caleb leaving past behind and starting new. The story grips your attention from the very beginning and holds it to the very end.<br><br><b>"Who am I?<br>Well, that’s what I’m trying to figure out. I was a whore in my youth, a killer since my adolescence, and a monster as a man. I am the man who kidnapped Livvie. I am the man who held her in a dark room for weeks. But, most importantly, I am the man she loves."</b><br><br>Nothing big happens in this story. Caleb and Livvie already got their happy ending. We've read Livvie's point of view, and now, Caleb tells us his. And it's freaking brilliant!<br>Their first meeting after a year isn't very pleasant.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391099679ra/8331071.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And who can blame Livvie? WTF Caleb? I would have done the same thing :-). But OMG it's hard to hate him. In so many ways he is still the same, but you also get to see his softer side (Yeah, I know, who knew he had one :-)).<br><b>
  <blockquote>"I know I can't ease our past. I can't promise you I'm a completely different person. I'm messed up in ways most people can't possibly understand, but I care about you. I had to find you and tell you you're the only thing I care about anymore</blockquote>
</b><br>You get to see how far they've come since their first meeting. Their second-first meeting is hard on both of them. Both of them are hurt, confused and unsure, but that thing that drew them together is still there. <br>There is no unnecessary drama. Yes, there is a lot of questions, but they both are willing to meet the other one halfway. That is what was so amazing about this book. <br><br>When they finally got to that "We are gonna be okay" place, it was joy to read. It was both fun and sad to. Fun because.... Because they both have a very kinky side to them. C. J. Roberts knows how to keep readers entertained :-D. It was nice to see Livvie having a little bit of power for once :-).<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1435505160ra/15354207.gif" width="390" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">.<br><br>The biggest surprise of all was Livvie, and her ability to forgive Caleb. Don't get me wrong, I like Livvie, loved her from the very beginning, but her strength and how understanding she was amazed me. It's impossible not to love her. I understand why Caleb was struggling so much. He wanted to the right thing, but how could you let go of someone like her?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1435505160ra/15354208.gif" width="390" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Caleb still has his kink on, but he is not the same man we got to meet in the first book. He is thoughtful and considerate when it comes to Livvie. It's not easy. He lived in that dark hole for a very long time, but f@ck me if he doesn't try to be the man that she deserves. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1435505160ra/15354209.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Livvie, you kinky kinky girl :-). It was nice to see her having some power. Although sometimes I wasn't sure who was on top, there was no mistake that she was Caleb's equal. There were many situations where she gladly gave up the control, but only because she knew she could trust him. And it was oh-so-pleasurable to read :-).<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1435505430ra/15354249.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Fantastic read. Writing is superb, amazing character development. Although I'm sad that Caleb's and Livvie's story is over, I can't wait for C. J. Roberts next book.<br><b>
  <blockquote>------------------<br>I just want to say one last thing. On the release day of TDD3 there was a mistake done by either amazon or Roberts herself, and it resulted in readers getting the draft instead of the finished copy of the book. I had to wait the whole day before I got the finished version of the book. Waiting was excruciating :). When I finally found out that the full book was available I decided to read the draft first. Why? because Roberts posted following message on her Facebook page: <i>"My stomach hurts. I am physically fucking ill thinking about all ppl reading that shitty draft. Fuuuuuuuuuck!"</i> I refused to believe that it was that bad. So, I decided to read it to see for myself. And let me tell you what. If every writer could write a draft at least half as "bad" as Roberts draft, there would be at least 4 star reviews from me every.single.time!</blockquote>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="16967596897824270415" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4388234780940484547">First let me say... I LOVED the Dark Duet! I found this series because it was often compared to mine. As C.J. has stated - a VERY unfair comparison. The Dark Duet and Epilogue are erotic, mine are not. But - we do have a kind of "mind-fuck" in common. Now, with that said... I LOVED the angst produced in the Dark Duet! I couldn't sleep, I HAD to know what would happen next.<br/><br/>Epilogue is just what it promised to be - Caleb's POV AFTER (thus the title) the end of Seduced in the Dark. I knew the endin</span>
  <span id="freeText4388234780940484547" style="display:none">First let me say... I LOVED the Dark Duet! I found this series because it was often compared to mine. As C.J. has stated - a VERY unfair comparison. The Dark Duet and Epilogue are erotic, mine are not. But - we do have a kind of "mind-fuck" in common. Now, with that said... I LOVED the angst produced in the Dark Duet! I couldn't sleep, I HAD to know what would happen next.<br /><br />Epilogue is just what it promised to be - Caleb's POV AFTER (thus the title) the end of Seduced in the Dark. I knew the ending, yet I continually worried something unforeseen would occur! **ANGST** (I won't tell you if it does or not, you need to find out for yourself!) <br /><br />I loved watching Caleb's inner struggles and transformation. It gives me hope for redemption! Well done C.J.! Thanks for this intimate look inside Caleb and Livie's / James and Sophie's relationship! <br /><br />I'm gonna fan fic in my own head about their future! Well, I already did. And I have a big smile on my face!!!<br /><br /><b>EDIT: 6/24/13</b> I don't know how I missed it, but I just read the alternate ending of Epilogue on C.J's goodreads page. It has been over a week since I read Epilogue and the alternate ending left me with tears in my eyes, a lump in my throat, and a huge smile on my face! Thanks C.J! Those three words made the entire story - all three books even better (if that were possible!). I always say I'm not a romantic, but maybe I'm wrong! </span>

<div id="review_532740795" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/532740795" />
    <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister"><img alt="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486056026p2/4971692.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/532740795?book_show_action=true">Feb 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister">Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer532740795" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7770602869712443570"><b>*3 So-So Stars*</b><br/><br/> This story is written entirely from Caleb's emotional perspective. As the title suggests, this is not a re-telling of the first two stories, but a conclusion that offers sporadic flashbacks into Caleb's dark past. While I didn't necessarily <i>dislike</i> this addition, I found it extremely inconsistent with the overall tone of the story. <br/><br/><i>Epilogue</i> opens with Caleb inviting us into his world—generously letting us step into his twisted and tortured mind. He speaks directly to the reader i</span>
  <span id="freeText7770602869712443570" style="display:none"><b>*3 So-So Stars*</b><br><br> This story is written entirely from Caleb's emotional perspective. As the title suggests, this is not a re-telling of the first two stories, but a conclusion that offers sporadic flashbacks into Caleb's dark past. While I didn't necessarily <i>dislike</i> this addition, I found it extremely inconsistent with the overall tone of the story. <br><br><i>Epilogue</i> opens with Caleb inviting us into his world—generously letting us step into his twisted and tortured mind. He speaks directly to the reader in a very personal manner, which I adored. Although I was happy to see that Caleb wasn't spontaneously cured of his emotional demons, I must admit, it wasn't at all what I expected.<br><br> I understand time has passed and both Caleb and Livvie have changed—but there were many moments where Caleb's character felt too different from his original persona. Rather than appearing as a broken man evolving, he came across as two separate characters, and I couldn't help getting tripped up by the blatant disconnect. <br><br>I also had mixed emotions over the way Caleb and Livvie were portrayed in a domestic, 'normal' setting. The fact that they were attempting their shot at normalcy was heartwarming, inspiring, and strange to witness all at the same time. Some things are just better left unsaid, and I feel the Dark Duet was too intense and exquisitely twisted to turn around and attempt a conventional aftermath where Caleb watches Harry Potter and plays Rock Band with quirky, upbeat friends. Not to say that I'd prefer seeing these characters bask in misery, but it didn't feel genuine no matter how hard I willed it to.<br><br>That said, we do often see Caleb in a state of despair, fighting to extinguish his old ways--and he does achieve much redemption while doing so. Livvie struggles to let go of the pain he has caused her and remains a solid support system for Caleb. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>I was learning that happiness also presents new ways to suffer. Misery, I understand. Happiness is terrifying.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>I really liked the design of this story and how it was constructed to reveal Caleb writing <i>his</i> own book for us. This author has a unique and beautiful way with words and my favorite parts in this story were the glimpses of Livvie's touching writing. The amazing Duet books will remain forever with me; they dared me to leap out of my comfort zone and I have found many more beautiful reads because of that!<br><br>All-in-all, this was a decent, somewhat uneventful, but tender epilogue that concluded a truly stunning series. <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2mh7uop" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="50" width="50" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380347313i/701667.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>
  <u>Book Stats:</u>
</b><br><b>▪	 Genre/Category:</b> Dark Erotica<br><b>▪	 Steam Caliber:</b> Maximum steam<br><b>▪ Romance:</b> Complicated, but evolving. Not entirely convincing. <br><b>▪	 Characters:</b> Showed tremendous growth; at times, characters felt <i>too</i> altered. <br><b>▪	 Plot:</b> While still battling their demons, Caleb and Livvie make a genuine attempt at a 'normal' relationship. <br><b>▪ Writing:</b> Superb, dark, and intense. Author excels at engaging the reader. <br><b>▪ POV:</b> 1st Person: Caleb's epilogue<br><b>▪	 Cliffhanger:</b> None<br><br><a href="http://prettywordsbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412050368i/11316768.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Pretty-Words-Book-Blog/860331017317983" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height='“40"' width="150" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413062455i/11461733._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1760878513?book_show_action=true">Oct 31, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bibi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bibi" href="/user/show/33411728-bibi">Bibi</a>
