<div id="review_525506295" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/525506295" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/525506295?book_show_action=true">Feb 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer525506295" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17718322577992969486"><b>ETA: Alternate ending posted by C.J. Roberts on 6/18/13...I've put it under the spoiler incase you don't want to see it! </b><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[<br/><br/>EPILOGUE (ALTERNATE)<br/><br/>So, here we are at the end. Was it good for you? It was for me. I suppose in the end that’s all that really matters. I know that’s selfish, but you know I’m selfish and you love me anyway.<br/><br/>For what it’s worth, I think I might actually miss you.<br/><br/>Will you miss me? <br/><br/>Will you cry? <br/><br/>If you do, please drink a tear for me and know that I never meant to </span></span>
  <span id="freeText17718322577992969486" style="display:none"><b>ETA: Alternate ending posted by C.J. Roberts on 6/18/13...I've put it under the spoiler incase you don't want to see it! </b><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br><br>EPILOGUE (ALTERNATE)<br><br>So, here we are at the end. Was it good for you? It was for me. I suppose in the end that’s all that really matters. I know that’s selfish, but you know I’m selfish and you love me anyway.<br><br>For what it’s worth, I think I might actually miss you.<br><br>Will you miss me? <br><br>Will you cry? <br><br>If you do, please drink a tear for me and know that I never meant to cause you pain. Our parting is no cause to fret. In the words of Frank Herbert, “There is no real ending. It’s just the place where you stop the story.”<br><br>Livvie and I go on. We still live and have adventures.<br><br>Will we see each other again? I don’t have the answer to that. Life has caught me to expect the unexpected and it’s a lesson I learn over and again. Suffice to say – I hope so.<br><br>To be perfectly honest, I’ve gone around and around trying to find the perfect ending to this novel I never intended to write. In the end, I’ve come to the conclusion that there wasn’t anything wrong with the way Livvie ended things. Her epilogue was short, but it captured the essence of our story: Survival is the most important thing. It affords us the chance to live and to find all of the things that make living worthwhile. I found redemption. I found forgiveness. I found love.<br><br>That said, Livvie did a beautiful job with the ending and I can think of no greater tribute than to end this book as she wrote it (with my helpful commentary along the way of course). Submitted for your heartbreak, I present: The Epilogue (2.0)<br><br>James swallowed thickly as he stared at the words on the screen. Sophia had written a very tragic love story, but it was a love story just the same. She had been very generous to him, painting a far better picture of the man he had been than he would have. (I think we’ve learned this is absolutely true.) She’d been working for weeks, sequestered in her little room upstairs. He wasn’t allowed in there, and though he didn’t like it, he respected Sophia’s wishes. He respected all her wishes these days. (Because I’m the best boyfriend ever! Sorry, Rubio.)<br><br>Several hours ago, she’d flown into the kitchen and thrown her arms around him.<br><br>“Why are you smiling, Kitten? Did you finally finish?” James asked.<br><br>“Yes! I finished,” she said and followed up with a little dance. (I love the little dance.) She’d immediately dragged him upstairs and planted him in front of the laptop so he could start reading. There wasn’t another chair, so she’d gotten down on her knees and rested her head on his knee. (She lies; she just likes kneeling at my feet.)<br><br>As he read, he stroked her hair. James had been scared to read everything from Sophia’s point of view, but he was glad he’d made it through and discovered just how Sophia remembered everything. She loved him, he was sure of it, and while he still didn’t think he deserved it, he was happy about it nonetheless. (This is entirely true.)<br><br>He once again gazed on her sleeping form, unable to resist shifting her hair away from her face and behind her ear. Her mouth was slack, and he was sure she had drooled on him, but it didn’t matter. She was the most beautiful thing he had ever seen. He couldn’t help but stroke her. He loved the soft noises she made when he did. He didn’t deserve her. He never did (also true).<br><br>She’d been with him for over a year now, and secretly he always hoped she would tire of him and decide to leave. (I didn’t hope—I feared.) She told him she loved him often, (I’ll give this to her. She did tell me she loved me often—not with her words, but with her deeds) and each time, it cut him down to his core. He didn’t deserve her love (no, I don’t). He couldn’t bring himself to pretend he did (no, I can’t).<br><br>When he’d learned she’d been writing their story, he helped her in any way he could. It was his outlet as much as hers. He needed to see it in black and white – the pain he put her through, the monster he had been. He never wanted to forget what he could never allow himself to become again (true).<br><br>Since the night Sophia had met him at the Paseo, the night he had decided to leave everything behind and integrate into mainstream society, so much of him had changed. Away from the horrors of his youth, away from blood and vengeance, he was just – James.<br><br>At first, he’d had no idea what to do with himself. All around him, real life was happening, and he was a spectator. What did he know about meeting people in cafés? About having friends that weren’t killers? (I love you, Livvie.)<br><br>But at night, in the dark, when he found he couldn’t sleep because the world felt suddenly too big – there was Sophia (yes).<br><br>Whenever he thought about running away and returning to the life he knew, he thought about the day he’d given her the note. She’d burst into tears and run away from the café. He’d thought she would call the FBI, and he’d been prepared to go to prison if they were the ones to meet him at the Paseo. (It sounds silly… now.)<br><br>Instead, she had met him there. She stood, looking like a goddess among commoners. Her hair lay in soft waves down her back, occasionally being picked up by the breeze. She wore a black halter dress that hugged her breasts and bared her back. She also wore incredibly tall heels. They were dangerous, considering the cobbled streets. She’d wanted him to know she was a grown woman, and she wasn’t afraid of him anymore. (I can still picture this in my mind.)<br><br>He approached her from across the square. He was nervous. He wore jeans and a black cashmere sweater. The sleeves were pushed up to his forearms. He wanted her to know he was different. He didn’t want to hurt her anymore.<br><br>Her back was to him as he approached, but the breeze suddenly died and she turned when she heard his steps approaching.<br><br>There had been no words. He simply stood in front of her with his hands in his pockets. Her breath caught, and for a while she only stared at him. She stepped closer, and he almost took a step back – but didn’t. She was suddenly very close, and he couldn’t help but inhale her scent and close his eyes. (I love the way she smells.) She touched his shirt and pulled him down. His head swam. (It did!) Then she kissed him, and it was all that needed to be said.<br><br>He moved to Barcelona so she could still attend university. They never talked about the past. When people asked them how they met, she was quick to intercept the question and respond. They had met at the Paseo de Colon. (If only it had been so simple.)<br><br>When they made love, he was surprised to discover Sophia’s tastes had evolved. She wanted him to spank her. She wanted him to bind her arms. He felt sick about it at first. Her proclivities were obviously his fault. Still, their games turned him on to the point of physical pain. (They still do.)<br><br>He felt villainous, but what was done was done, and now he would do everything he could to give her what she wanted. He owed her much. Besides, it wasn’t always rough. Sometimes it was vanilla – and he liked that too (very much).<br><br>Carefully, James lifted Sophia into his arms and carried her to their bedroom. He laid her down on the bed, smiling as she shifted around, seeking some way to get comfortable. He undressed and got in bed next to her. Just touching her made him hard. He owed her so much. (Only everything.)<br><br>Suddenly overwhelmed, he held her impossibly tight. She whimpered and whined until her eyes opened and she stared up at his face. “Oh my god, what’s wrong?” she asked and stroked his distressed face. <br><br>“I love you,” he whispered. <br><br>“I love you, too,” she replied. Sophia’s eyes welled up with tears and she tilted her face toward his. <br><br>She kissed him so passionately, so sweetly, that James thought if she never kissed him again, this was the kiss he always wanted to remember (it still is).<br><br>I could never write an ending better than the one Livvie gave you, but I’ll leave you with this: Once upon a time I saved Livvie. She’s been saving me ever since.<br><br>The End <br><br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>I LOVE the last line! ♥ </b><br><br>and here's a video she posted that explains things:<br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=gy0z5JXhAK4&amp;feature=youtu.be">http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=gy0z5J...</a><br><br>******************************************************<br><br><b>My Review:</b><br><br>The Epilogue...the ending...the happy ever after, or not? Well, we begged for it and now we have it...for better or worse. <br><br>This story is <i>exactly</i> what I thought it would be and everything I didn't think it would be. I wanted to know what happened to Livvie and Caleb, I wanted to know if they got a happy ever after and I wanted Caleb's POV. What I wasn't expecting is how much I would miss Livvie and how raw and exposed we would find Caleb. <br><br><b>
  <u>My Caleb</u>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379793741i/582142._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Both Livvie and Caleb have changed...how could they not? But we get to experience with them, how and <i>if</i> the new Livvie and Caleb can work. And it's a little unnerving seeing the two sides of them mesh together. Livvie suggested that there are times for them to be Sophia and James and times for them to be Livvie and Caleb and I thought that was ingenious. But I like how Caleb said it best:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379793741i/582141.png" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And of course, we get many amazing, steamy sex scenes from Kitten and Sexy...that chemistry is still there and it was sooo much more because they were able to just love each other. <br><br>I did enjoy all of Caleb's firsts and I have to hand it to Livvie and how well she incorporated things. I was a little surprised at first at Caleb's go with the flow "vibe", I really thought he would be involved in all kinds of things. But it worked for him and I think his "exercise program" was a big help as was his construction projects. <br><br>I really enjoyed the parts that Rubio and Claudia brought to the story. I got a kick out of all the things that Caleb thought and how he came around on some things. Who knew that Caleb could be so funny...in a serious and scary sort of way! <br><br>My favorite, <i>favorite</i> thing was another first...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379793741i/582143._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>...my heart just went out to that little boy and the man that he has become. <br><br>And the ending? Well, curses CJR....how could you end a book like that?? But as Frank Herbert was quoted, "There is no real ending. It's just the place where you stop the story." (for now) <br><br><br>Favorite quotes: <br><br>♥ “I missed you every day, Kitten. Every. F*cking. Day.”<br><br>♥ “No, Kitten. I’m not okay,” I whispered. “I don’t know how long it’s going to take for me to <i>be</i> okay. I just know that as long as you’re with me, there’s a chance that one day… I might be.”<br><br>♦ (I use feet for your benefit, but you should really learn metric, America)... <i>I loved all Caleb's little comments to the reader!</i><br><br>♦ "I'd never considered myself socially retarded until that moment."<br><br>♥ "Mine."<br><br>♦ "Livvie and I will never wear matching outfits. No!"... <i>LOL!</i><br><br>♦ "Sexy's Kung-fu Boo-Boo kit."</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14386067531167328454">The sex was...Hot. Hot. Hot.<br/><br/>Post-trauma Livvie and Caleb as a couple outside of the bedroom, however...<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408923i/800334.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>There's something about seeing the "after" that tends to mess with the entire experience. Sometimes I'd rather be left on my own to imagine what happens next. Watching people in a domesticated setting kills some of the mystery. <i>Example : Any Fever series fans remember the travesty that was Barrons <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[grilling <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>?</i><br/><br/>But I was curious enough to read this and it was still hot</span>
  <span id="freeText14386067531167328454" style="display:none">The sex was...Hot. Hot. Hot.<br><br>Post-trauma Livvie and Caleb as a couple outside of the bedroom, however...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408923i/800334.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>There's something about seeing the "after" that tends to mess with the entire experience. Sometimes I'd rather be left on my own to imagine what happens next. Watching people in a domesticated setting kills some of the mystery. <i>Example : Any Fever series fans remember the travesty that was Barrons <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[grilling <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>?</i><br><br>But I was curious enough to read this and it was still hot when it needed to be, so *thumbs up* for that.<br><br>I'm glad that Caleb wasn't "miraculously" normal after all he'd been through. Do I think he was less creepy than he should have been, given how twisted he was before? Possibly? But the author did a good job of balancing who he was before and who he is now without tipping too far in either direction. There had to be some healing and some semblance of humanity poking around in there, or the entire epilogue would have been pointless. But if he'd all of a sudden become a completely level-headed and mainstream-functioning individual, it would have killed the point of books 1 and 2. <br><br>Overall, I don't gather that there was a necessary epilogue happening here. Book 2 ended the story at a good point. But fans who can't get enough of these characters will probably enjoy checking this short book out.<br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer526054725" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10302623381767138155"><a href='http://s1269.photobucket.com/user/deathlysilenceoriginal/media/415b23a6-270a-427f-ac11-cff2ef10a7a6_zps9856ffcc.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

  <u>Do not read this review if you haven’t read the previous books :)</u>

This journey had its ups and downs but I never thought that it would end in this way .I'm really glad I read these books because characters as Livvie should be mimicked. What I mean is that even though she was manipulated so badly she managed to stay strong on her feet again. It was difficult to forget him , to erase her past but what about Caleb? This book has all the answers about these </span>

</a><br><b>

</b><br><br>It's really sad when a story ends. This journey had its ups and downs but I never thought that it would end in this way .I'm really glad I read these books because characters as Livvie should be mimicked. What I mean is that even though she was manipulated so badly she managed to stay strong on her feet again. It was difficult to forget him , to erase her past but what about Caleb? This book has all the answers about these two people. I'm very happy that the author decided to write the Epilogue .<br>If she hadn’t I'm sure I'll still be wondering how they would deal with their lives.<br><a href="http://s1269.photobucket.com/user/deathlysilenceoriginal/media/e2bc30a7-e182-4709-8a10-d92afed3c328_zps89a39489.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br>Caleb's void roars in life and the only person who can make him whole again is Livvie . He has to find her , be with her !<br>Their meeting isnt mentioned in SITD and I have to admit that I laughed a lot.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380408085ra/798004.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380408085ra/798005.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><p>
  <b>She hit me so hard my damn eyes were watering (I was not crying—eyes water. I think we all know I’m a badass and I don’t cry).</b>
</p><br><br>Livvie is willing to try again with him.Start everything from the beginning , be a normal couple , but is that even possible since they're both fucked up in the worst ways?<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400751i/777039.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It is very nice to see these two trying.Livvie is really good in pretending that is a normal college girl.Caleb on the other hand left me laughing so hard.Oh god he was such a caveman.I guess some habits *clears throat* cant be forgotten .<br><br>Around her he is soft and we can see that he is a human after all. I always thought that he was a f***ing b@stard.I dont know how the author did this but I ended up liking him . <br><br>I dont know what's wrong with me but I cant review this book so I'm stopping here.I loved it and that's all it matters.These two characters will definitely stay with me forever.<br><p><i>Can I say goodbye?</i><br>Not really.</p><br><br>Ok, the epilogue confused me a lot.<br>I want to believe that we arent saying a goodbye forever but that we will see them again.<br>I'm looking forward to more :)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380408085ra/798006.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><a href="http://s1269.photobucket.com/user/deathlysilenceoriginal/media/21c0ed5c-e052-4c4a-b6b9-fb072b69fe77_zps85d634f3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

I don't want to read pages and pages of dull dinner parties and playing Guitar Hero (or Rock Band? I forget, I was too busy yawning). This book was taking the bad ass of all bad asses (Caleb) and making him do horribly mundane things. I don't want to see Caleb cooking freaking dinner or making puns or going clothes shopping. This book was like turning on all the lights during a one night stand and finding out that the person you are hooking up with has oozing boils on his face... just horrifying. <br><br>To boot, nothing happened in this book! I was expected some major drama and got NOTHING. I wanted some tension, some adrenaline but instead I just got never-ending chapters of whiny complaining. <br><br><i>Le sigh</i> At least the sex was hot (<b>smoking</b> at times, hence the extra star). However, I still just wanted them to go balls to the wall and this was just so wishy washy. In the end, I actually wish that I ended their story on book two. It was perfect. Now my memory of Livvie and Caleb is marred by this... disaster. <br></span>

<div id="review_559517018" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/559517018" />
    <a title="Shannon The Show Stopper " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16205457-shannon-the-show-stopper"><img alt="Shannon The Show Stopper " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388257799p2/16205457.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/559517018?book_show_action=true">Mar 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shannon The Show Stopper " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shannon The Show Stopper " href="/user/show/16205457-shannon-the-show-stopper">Shannon The Show Stopper </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer559517018" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5543384614067902956">I was never able to be fully drawn into this book like I was the first two. As much as I wanted Caleb and Livvie to move past their experience and integrate into society, I'm not sure I actually wanted to watch it happen. I loved Seduce in the Dark so much and I think it was truly the masterpiece of the series. So of course since I loved the characters so much, I wanted more. Now that I got what I thought I wanted, I'm not so sure. <br/><br/>Here's an example of why this book was just 'off' for me.<br/><br/><b>Caleb<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413152ra/813095.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>My</b></span>
  <span id="freeText5543384614067902956" style="display:none">I was never able to be fully drawn into this book like I was the first two. As much as I wanted Caleb and Livvie to move past their experience and integrate into society, I'm not sure I actually wanted to watch it happen. I loved Seduce in the Dark so much and I think it was truly the masterpiece of the series. So of course since I loved the characters so much, I wanted more. Now that I got what I thought I wanted, I'm not so sure. <br><br>Here's an example of why this book was just 'off' for me.<br><br><b>Caleb<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413152ra/813095.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My reaction<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/526208.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413152ra/813096.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Then my reaction to my reaction<br><br><a href="http://s1341.photobucket.com/user/shannon_phillips6/media/Reactions/tumblr_lpfrp9bT9R1qib9ks_zps3a43d3f8.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/541486.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_lpfrp9bT9R1qib9ks_zps3a43d3f8.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>Do I want to think of Caleb as<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413152ra/813097.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404489ra/787119.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yeah, that is just one example and the book was full of super cutesy stuff that just didn't really fit with the series. You know what they say about too much of a good thing. </b></span>
  <a data-text-id="5543384614067902956" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText399520673847303676" style="display:none">Actually it didn't work for me<br>It almost felt.......<br>I don't know , Boring ?<br>It's a short book at least for my standards but still I had a hard time to finish it<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1599727547ra/30086382.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Also <br>I had some major issues which put me off at the first place<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1599727547ra/30086383.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>If I don't pin point it , it will bother me a lot 😑<br><br>{ If you haven't read book 1 and 2 then don't proceed it will be spoilerish}<br><br>So-<br><br><b>1.Double Standards aka mother of hypocrisy :</b> <br>Sweetheart , you are allowed to cheat on her ; when you are having a break or you are on your "redemption period" you can sleep with other women with the side remark "they didn't mean anything because they are not Livvie " <br>WTF dude ? <br>What is it ? <br>and She can't even see a man ? This time obviously it was consensual but still it made me uncomfortable .<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1599727547ra/30086385.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>3.Red Flag</b><br>Guiltily admitting possessiveness , protectiveness , having a claim on your girl is always a turn on for me . I promise.”I didn’t	mention the part where I’d lose my	fucking mind. Maybe not.I was only<br>better when I was living for her.I felt like	a time-bomb."</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1599727547ra/30086386.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I mean<br>RUN SIS RUN! <br>WHAT ARE YOU WAITING FOR?<br><br><b>4. Pet</b><br>I mean stop ! <br>Stop calling her that! She is not your slave <br>I was feeling offended on her behalf 😒<br><br>In short I was better off without Book 3 <br><br>I think he needs monthly psychiatrist visits<br>Whatever at least Livvie Slapped him quite a few times so I am happy 😂<br><br>If you guys are up for quick SMUT read which you will get here ( plenty ) then here you go. <br>Unfortunately SMUT is not my thing unless I feel the chemistry, respect and affection from the Male Lead if that makes sense 🙄<br><br>From Chapter 11 things got comparatively<br>better for me.<br><br><b>I think I was seeking for his closure and apology more than the sexy stuffs</b><br><br>Also when it is a 15 chaptered book and I didn't like 10 chapters of it then it's not cool at all.<br><br>I will again emphasise on my statement if you are not fond of Dark Romance then it is not your thing<br><br>you could love this book <br>or<br>you will absouletly despise it<br>there is no middle ground<br><br><b>then again I think I crave for darkness time to time to appreciate the brightness more.   <span id="freeText13194610048961275647" style="display:none">10.0000000 Stars Masterpiece..<br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380412432ra/810982.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Yes after all the waiting and the drama with the draft(I'm not complaining it gave me time to re-read the first two books)i finally finished it..<br>WOW!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/468453.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I love James(good) and Caleb(evil) with the same amount..<br>I actually found Caleb yes the one we all know being so sweet..<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/588390.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Don't judge me just yet! I'm crazy Anna(mama bear) and Rosa already pointed out that when i told them he is a cutie-pie.. <br>I know you 'll never thought of him like that but please consider this: A super hot guy 6,4 feet tall, throwing a tanrum inside an elevator because he is scared for life..by some kids bouncing around..<br>Yes the same guy who firstly kills and then talks.. <br><br>Joking aside it's refreshing seeing him unsure, afraid and out of his league in so many levels..<br>He never had a normal life and the way he is being introduced to so many things it's really captivating.. The movies, the games, the friends.. The birthdays..Yes those in particular.. And the dreams..<br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380412432ra/810983.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Even after they found each other their relationship keeps moving, growing, changing and becoming stronger..<br>How can anyone hold a grudge when those two find in each other their missing half..<br>And who would still be upset with him while he plays Super Mario like the six year old he never had the chance to be..<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380412432ra/810984.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Caleb is working hard with himself, he screws up a bit but he never gives up.. He comes to terms with many issues and tries to resolve the rest.. They heal each other and Livvie has made excellent work with herself..<br>Caleb's witt and his snarky comments whith an honest inner voice and Livvie's braziness, humor and ability to diffuse the time bomb that he is made the book light and easier to read..<br>I also enjoyed Rubio and Claudia..<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380412432i/810985.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This is why we read books for the occasional rare finding of a read that will blow up your mind stumble upon your shattered heart's little pieces and make you whole again..<br>Gifting you with a new perspective of your self and the world and the story your reading.. Take you to your limits and even further..<br>Conratulations CJ Roberts for the amazing conclusion to such an unbelievable series..<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/571533.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I would write my fav quotes but i decided against it.. They were too many..</span>

<div id="review_948647795" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/948647795" />
    <a title="Eda**" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6285155-eda"><img alt="Eda**" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1581410351p2/6285155.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/948647795?book_show_action=true">May 26, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Eda**" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Eda**" href="/user/show/6285155-eda">Eda**</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer948647795" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16419713859031037262"><br/><b>
  <i>** 3 "<u>#CalebIsWayBetterThanJames</u>" STARS **</i>
</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Tell me to stop and I will. Tell me you don't want me to pull your tights down and f*ck you up against this wall. Remind me of what a terrible person I am. Tell me I'm a sick bastard and you want me out of your life forever. Tell me I don't deserve you. Tell me all the things I already know."<br/>~ CALEB/JAMES</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380367914ra/720417.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I hate DNFing. I hate it, so I do it <b>VERY</b> rarely.<br/><br/>This is one of the seldom number of books that had pushed me to do it though when I fi</span>
  <span id="freeText16419713859031037262" style="display:none"><br><b>
  <i>** 3 "<u>#CalebIsWayBetterThanJames</u>" STARS **</i>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Tell me to stop and I will. Tell me you don't want me to pull your tights down and f*ck you up against this wall. Remind me of what a terrible person I am. Tell me I'm a sick bastard and you want me out of your life forever. Tell me I don't deserve you. Tell me all the things I already know."<br>~ CALEB/JAMES</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380367914ra/720417.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I hate DNFing. I hate it, so I do it <b>VERY</b> rarely.<br><br>This is one of the seldom number of books that had pushed me to do it though when I first read it.<br><br>But just because I hated to see a book from one of my favorite series on my shameful DNF list, I decided to give it another try now.<br><br><i>I'm glad I did.</i> I've missed <u>Caleb</u> and <u>Livvie</u>, so I was happy to read about them some more.<br><br>But I still think this book is <b>UNNECESSARY</b>.<br><br>The ending of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13612739.Seduced_in_the_Dark__The_Dark_Duet___2_" title="Seduced in the Dark (The Dark Duet, #2) by C.J. Roberts" rel="nofollow noopener">Seduced in the Dark</a> is <b>PERFECT</b>.<br><br><i>Why ruin it by dragging the story?</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416341446ra/11941020.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>Caleb</u> has come back for Livvie.<br><br><u>Livvie</u> has been waiting for Caleb.<br><br>Now they are finally together. Now they finally have a chance at happiness.<br><br><i>But it's not that easy to erase the past, the mistakes, the heartbreaks.</i><br><br>Caleb is having trouble being normal. He is having trouble being the man that Livvie needs him to be. He is having trouble being <u>James</u>.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>She was mine, and yet I couldn't touch her where it mattered. I couldn't touch her heart and force her to give me the things I had stupidly come to need. (...) Loving Livvie was like allowing myself to be peeled open and hollowed out. She made me weak. She made me vulnerable. She made me ache and long and hope for all the things that could never be mine.<br>~ CALEB/JAMES</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Livvie is having trouble trusting Caleb again. She is having trouble forgetting and forgiving. She is having trouble believing he can change, that he loves her, that he will never leave her again...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You are the best thing that's ever happened to me, Caleb. You're also the worst."<br>~ LIVVIE/SOPHIE</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><i>Will they be able to come over all the obstacles on their way to happiness?</i><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395028703ra/8937360.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1406229086ra/10522630.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_525975288" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/525975288" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/525975288?book_show_action=true">Feb 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=i-like-it-dark-and-twisted">i-like-it-dark-and-twisted</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer525975288" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8279745442851422198"><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408072i/797914._SY540_.jpg' width='380' height='420' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Is this fifteen chapter book worth the purchase and read? <b>ABSOLUTELY!</b><br/><br/><i>Epilogue</i> is told completely in Caleb/James pov which was...sarcastic/witty, heartbreaking, heart-warming and sexy. Caleb takes a reader through his two sides…Caleb and James and how he now is the combination of both men.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>"I am the man who kidnapped Livie. I am the man who held her in a dark room for weeks. I'm the one who tied her to a bedpost and beat her. I'm the one who nearly sold her into sexual slavery. But, most import</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText8279745442851422198" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408072i/797914._SY540_.jpg" width="380" height="420" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Is this fifteen chapter book worth the purchase and read? <b>ABSOLUTELY!</b><br><br><i>Epilogue</i> is told completely in Caleb/James pov which was...sarcastic/witty, heartbreaking, heart-warming and sexy. Caleb takes a reader through his two sides…Caleb and James and how he now is the combination of both men.<br><br><b>
  <i>"I am the man who kidnapped Livie. I am the man who held her in a dark room for weeks. I'm the one who tied her to a bedpost and beat her. I'm the one who nearly sold her into sexual slavery. But, most importantly, I am the man she loves. She loves me. It's quite sick, isn't it?"</i>
</b> <br><br>Readers experience Caleb's inner thoughts and his desire to be with Livie and find a way to fit into her life. Livie is a survivor. She has not only survived Caleb but all the mind bending time she spent with Agent Reed in book two. This story starts right where <i>Seduced in the Dark </i> left our couple. This story shows the ups and downs they experienced to make their relationship work. <br><br>Caleb learns that there are many more sides to the girl he held captured in the dark. The day-to-day Livie loves movies, friends, holidays and a reader will enjoy Caleb becoming a good boyfriend. As these two find what works for them and their relationship stepping out from the dark into the light of day.<br><br>I only wanted one thing since book one – I wanted the girl at the bus stop to survive the horror that grabbed her out of her life. I feared that she would never survive both physically and mentally from the ordeal. She will forever be one of my favorite book heroines. Livie/Sophie ~You did it! <br><br><b>
  <i>"There is no real ending. It's just the place where you stop the story." ~ Frank Herbert"</i>
</b><br><br>I want to thank C.J. Roberts for this series. It will forever haunt me. <br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="8279745442851422198" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1128196898" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4800209895966243576"><b>"3 sexy stars"</b><br/> <br/>Anything to do with Livvie, Caleb and C J Roberts I absolutely love and Epilogue was no exception. Yes! I realize I rated it <i>‘3 stars’</i> not because I hated it or it was boring but the author is to blame here, Yes Mrs Roberts I blame you if my future dark/angst/romance reads fall short because you have created one of the best scintillating story of love, betrayal, faith and survival in <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1125283864?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>‘Seduced in the Dark’</a> which will forever be my top favorite. <blockquote>
<b>“I’m writing this because you begged</b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText4800209895966243576" style="display:none"><b>"3 sexy stars"</b><br> <br>Anything to do with Livvie, Caleb and C J Roberts I absolutely love and Epilogue was no exception. Yes! I realize I rated it <i>‘3 stars’</i> not because I hated it or it was boring but the author is to blame here, Yes Mrs Roberts I blame you if my future dark/angst/romance reads fall short because you have created one of the best scintillating story of love, betrayal, faith and survival in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1125283864?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">‘Seduced in the Dark’</a> which will forever be my top favorite. <blockquote>
<b>“I’m writing this because you begged.<br>You know how I love the begging”</b> </blockquote>This is a prolonged epilogue to an already written one in book 2 of this series said from Caleb’s POV. It’s a detailed version of their reunion after one year of separation.<br><br>Livvie even after moving to different country realizes her feelings for Caleb has not changed, she never moved on from the day he left without so much of saying how he feels or if he’s ever going to meet her again. Buried in his misery due to aftermath of betrayal from Rafiq and killing his only family, Caleb moves around the world righting his wrong in a path of salvation but never finds it as he knows it lies with his kitten. Almost after a year Caleb tracks down Livvie and sends her a note to meet him, but their reunion doesn’t go as expected. Livvie does miss him though she is not the same girl who obeys him or cling to him for her survival, it leaves Caleb to save their relationship and be a better man for Livvie and win her heart, gain her trust by loving her back.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418461245i/12792976._SX540_.jpg" width="410" height="330" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Caleb tries hard alright! He does everything in his power to make things work out for them but it’s not as easy as he first thought. Even when love brought them together there are so many things that can rip them apart. Livvie finds it hard to trust him since he once broke her heart and left her to face their reality alone. There is part of her which always fears him, sees him as a monster he once was. Caleb never had a normal life but living with Livvie made him to see different shades to life, he’s still struggling with the demons of his past but also embraces his new found happiness and life to normalcy with Livvie and he has no intention to let it go. The only way for them to move forward is to let go the memories of their old life, make new one’s and be true to their feelings for one another.<blockquote>
<b>“I found redemption.<br>I found forgiveness. <br>I found love.<br>- Caleb”</b> </blockquote> <b>Rating clarification</b>-There was no drama no angst and no Caleb’y allure to his new persona and I missed him terribly. James on other hand was thoughtful, sweet, funny and <i>‘best boyfriend’</i> as Sophie would say. There was a detailed account of day to day activities which was quite a drag and most of the times I felt these two characters are totally different from one’s we have come to know and love. <br><br>That being said, I still enjoyed this most deserved ending for Livvie and Caleb. And I’m so glad the author gave it from Caleb’s POV, we knew his dilemma from past two books but being in his head makes you see his struggle and understand his conflict very well. I seriously didn’t expect him to be so damn witty and funny, I loved their banters, their cute romantic moments and the very first birthday Caleb ever celebrated was heart touching. I have to say this since it occupies major part of the book-“SEX” is like freaking HOT and that was the only time I got to see control freak, dominating, horny badass side of Caleb, gladly the author didn’t try to overshadow the story by filling it with sex scenes.<br><br><b>“Once upon a time I saved Livvie. She’s been saving me ever since.”</b><br><br><i>This is the story of second chance, healing, living and loving, a perfect conclusion to the perfect love story.</i></span>

<div id="review_525964299" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/525964299" />
    <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog"><img alt="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1554795448p2/3870376.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/525964299?book_show_action=true">Feb 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog">Jenny - TotallybookedBlog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer525964299" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12852560882928417400"><i>Who am I?<br/>Am I Caleb?<br/>Am I James?<br/><br/>I’ve often asked myself this very thing and have always come up with a different answer. Perhaps the only answer that can be truthful is to say, “I am both.”</i><br/><br/>Such was the beginning of Epilogue and with these words I was drawn back into the Dark Duet series. Those words crushed me for the man who was, and is, Caleb/James.<br/><br/>Being up close and personal with Caleb felt……. intimate. I experienced a connection and a love for Caleb the like in which I never have before – it </span>
  <span id="freeText12852560882928417400" style="display:none"><i>Who am I?<br />Am I Caleb?<br />Am I James?<br /><br />I’ve often asked myself this very thing and have always come up with a different answer. Perhaps the only answer that can be truthful is to say, “I am both.”</i><br /><br />Such was the beginning of Epilogue and with these words I was drawn back into the Dark Duet series. Those words crushed me for the man who was, and is, Caleb/James.<br /><br />Being up close and personal with Caleb felt……. intimate. I experienced a connection and a love for Caleb the like in which I never have before – it was as if Caleb was narrating his story to me personally. As if this beautiful, dangerous and damaged man was laying his inner most thoughts, fears and feelings bare… to <b>ME.</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Tell me I don’t deserve you. Tell me all the things I already know.”</i>
</b><br /><br />Caleb’s telling of his story touched me deeply and had me laughing with him, feeling happiness and sadness for him, whilst also experiencing a sense of anger both at him and with him. Stripping his emotions bare for all to see rendered me to tears and made want to reach out, touch his cheek, offer him assurance and urge him to continue. His humour charmed me and the power of Caleb’s voice culminated in emotions of every description to course through me.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“She wanted me. She wanted me as much as I wanted her…..”</i>
</b><br /><br />Caleb’s story always demanded to be told. Well I know I wanted to hear it – and who else but Caleb could make us understand and give us the answers we so desperately craved. There was much I desired to hear. Oh, don’t get me wrong, I was completely satisfied at the end of Seduced, but if I was going to be privy to Caleb’s narrative on how Livvie and Caleb arrived at the point at the end of Seduced …well, the opportunity was one I wasn’t going to miss!! From that point, a <i>want</i> to know became a need to know.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Fear is part of it.”</i>
</b><br /><br />Why Livvie? Why did he choose Livvie, and how was she to have such an effect on Caleb……how was she able to enter his heart and break down his defenses where others hadn’t. Who was Caleb now? Was he very different to the Caleb then? What feelings did he experience that night in September of 2010, the night he met Livvie at The Paseo. I needed to know it all!<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“It was only natural for her to wonder about the ways I hadn’t changed.”</i>
</b><br /><br />Well, I could not have been more impressed with the execution and conclusion of Caleb’s words in Epilogue if I tried. CJ Roberts has indeed done Caleb, and her readers proud.<br /><br />Caleb is an engaging, charming, sexy and witty narrator who completely captivated me. His is a story peppered with humour, inner conflict, cheekiness and honesty.<br /><br />Did Caleb slip effortlessly back into Livvie’s life or did he have to fight like he has never fought before? How had Livvie coped without Caleb during his absence and how did Livvie move on and make a life for herself?<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I always wondered—before—if you craved me like this. Did you?”</i>
</b><br /><br />We are afforded so much more than mere “answers” in Epilogue. CJ Roberts has written a raw tale in what I feel is an absolute must read for those of us who took Livvie and Caleb into our hearts. To bear witness to the struggle, the turmoil, the fun, the sensuality and the absolute passion between these two really is compelling reading and in no way constitutes <i>“an alternative pov”</i> tag.<br /><br />Epilogue does not simply fill in the gaps. It manages to give us an extension of the story where the reader experiences a journey so different and intoxicating it’s akin to feeling a new phase in the lives of Livvie and Caleb. Epilogue is a frank, gritty, passionate and emotional read where feelings are stripped raw and the narrative is told in an almost voyeuristic manner. <br /><br />Oh yeah, I admit it….there was a time or two I actually answered Caleb, such was the intimate nature in the way he conveyed his thoughts, as if he were conversing with me personally.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“No one knew who we were or what we had been through to get to that moment.”</i>
</b><br /><br />The sex is kinky and very, VERY hot …..oh and very, very consensual…..VERY consensual.<br />These two have been programmed in such a way that sex, the sex they enjoy, is very much a part of them as breathing. How they express and feel, so much is sexual and experiencing the emotion built into these scenes will leave you breathless. Yep readers, these two definitely know how to get your pulse racing!<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“No questions, Pet. You’ll like it. I promise. Or at the very least, I will.”</i>
</b><br /><br />As I said, the manner in which this story is told really does make one feel like a voyeur watching two people in their most private, intimate moments and with this came the heart crashing feelings of witnessing Caleb attempting to assimilate into Livvie’s life, trying to understand the woman she was to the woman she is, addressing his guilt and desperately wanting to be part of Livvie’s life.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“My feelings toward her were on the tip of my tongue. I’d been holding the words in since the moment I had watched her walk out of my life…”</i>
</b><br /><br />Livvie was a revelation. This girl who we all empathized with, hurt with and who made us feel so desperately for the girl who lost her youth and her innocence and who, at the hands of Caleb experienced the most harrowing, confusing and conflicting of situations and emotions…..how did Livvie survive and maintain the capacity to forgive and love? Or did she? Hers is an inner strength we admire greatly.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I want to ask you a few questions, Caleb, and I need for you to be completely honest with me. Can you do that?”</i>
</b><br /><br />I cannot urge readers enough to pick up and devour Epilogue as I did. To refer to Epilogue as merely <i>“Caleb’s pov”</i> would so far off the mark because Epilogue is, in fact, an extension of the story and an absolute <b>MUST READ</b>.<br /><br />CJ Roberts is an author who knows how to deliver a story. This author loves, deeply loves her characters and it shows. She has never shied from telling Caleb and Livvie’s story the way “they” want it told and has always remained true to her characters, even if that has been at the discomfort of the reader and for that I admire and respect her greatly.<br /><br />As a reader I love nothing more than to be tested. To be taken out of my comfort zone, to question my thought process and feel emotion to the point of tears and anger, to have my gut twisting and my heart aching….it’s what reading is all about for me and it’s bloody exhilarating. There’s nothing better, and I can tell you that has been my experience with every book in the Dark Duet Series and Epilogue is no exception.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Tell me I’m a sick bastard and you want me out of your life forever.”</i>
</b><br /><br />Epilogue is Caleb’s story and who better to trust with his story than the person who loves him most. CJ Roberts….. Caleb and I commend you. What a truly sensual, beautiful, emotional, provocative, passionate and raw story you and Caleb have given us.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I know, Pet. We’ve come a long way from there. Yet, here we are….”</i>
</b><br /><br />Caleb spoke, CJ answered and I listened.<br /><br />Caleb and Livvie, you own my heart. .<br /><br /><br /><i>ARC Supplied by author for an honest review </i></span>
  <a data-text-id="12852560882928417400" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer525421690" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16621713171543403797"><i>
  <b>“Well, first, I want to say I’m thankful for the food. I can’t wait to eat it. But, more importantly…I’m thankful that I’m here at all.”</b>
</i><br/><br/><br/>When I read that first book, I remember putting it aside at some point thinking that what I was witnessing was crazy. I felt like I was intruding on emotions that I had no business watching. And frankly that I would never be able to understand. So when I saw the above quote, my heart broke for her. She's not even 20 years old, for God's sake, and makes state</span>
  <span id="freeText16621713171543403797" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>“Well, first, I want to say I’m thankful for the food. I can’t wait to eat it. But, more importantly…I’m thankful that I’m here at all.”</b>
</i><br><br><br>When I read that first book, I remember putting it aside at some point thinking that what I was witnessing was crazy. I felt like I was intruding on emotions that I had no business watching. And frankly that I would never be able to understand. So when I saw the above quote, my heart broke for her. She's not even 20 years old, for God's sake, and makes statements with such subtlety knowing how lucky she is for having survived a fate that would have been her mental doom.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407989i/797551._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>
  <b>“I apologize, Livvie. I’ve apologized ad nauseum. I fuck you when you want to be fucked. I play nice for your friends. I wait for you to come home because I have nothing more to do. You’ve become my whole life! Meanwhile, you’re writing about me. You still see me as the man I was. You still see the killer; beautiful on the outside and hideous on the inside. Why are you with me? Why am I trying so hard to be someone else when all I’ll ever be to you is the man who ruined your life?”</b>
</i><br><br><br>I mean how do you forgive the person who practically destroyed you, broke you down, put you back together, saved you and then left you? Not only how do you forgive him, but how do you trust him?<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407989i/797552._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>
  <b>“You love me?” she said as she looked into my eyes. “When did you come to the realization? Was it when I told you I loved you and you said it was cute? Or maybe it was after I killed a man? Possibly, when I begged you not to leave me at the border? “Did you realize you loved me while I was alone in the hospital and weeping over you? When did you shout your love from the rooftops, Caleb? I couldn’t hear you. I was too busy trying to fucking breathe without you. I was busy convincing everyone around me I wasn’t crazy for defending my kidnapper. So, remind me. When did you say the words? I’ll be sure to go back in me and comfort the broken girl you le in your wake. Your love can comfort her, because I’m not the same person anymore."</b>
</i> <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407989i/797553.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Feelings are possible. Desire is possible. Even love is possible. But trust?This is a long and exhausting path but one that is necessary. Seeing Caleb reading about Livvie's experience through her eyes was one nice, vicious bitchslap that woke him up.<br><br><br><i>
  <b>“I’ve learned to breathe without you. I’ve learned there’s no one in this life I can trust. It isn’t the fact you read my words. I don’t care about that. I would have shown you eventually. It’s the note you left. It’s now. It’s knowing that at any moment you’re going to run off and leave me again. How can I tell you I love you? How could I survive it again?”</b>
</i><br><br><br>But what I seem to agree with is that, two negatives may make a positive. So make this positive count. Turn Caleb into James and the dog into a man. Because after all that torture, there has to be a sliver of hope. Just a thread is enough to bind to broken shells together. To fill two empty voids. To write an epilogue to a story.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407989i/797554._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>
  <b>I imagined myself as her Prince Charming. I was not a monster. I was worthy. My heart was not an empty husk; it was engorged with blood and feeling. Buried inside Livvie, my heart responded to the truth in her eyes: I love you too, Livvie.</b>
</i> <br><br></span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=male-pov">male-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=bdsm">bdsm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=hells-yeah-alphas">hells-yeah-alphas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=fav-book-boyfriend">fav-book-boyfriend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=mind-f-ck">mind-f-ck</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer525532033" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10637983867368688285"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405576i/790308._SX540_.jpg' width='125' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>♥♥♥ 5 STARS ♥♥♥</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408006i/797686._SY540_.jpg' height='500' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>I LOVED IT!!</b> I am so glad we got to see Caleb's side!<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br/><br/>"Who am I?<br/>Am I Caleb?<br/>Am I James?<br/>I've often asked myself this very thing and have always come up with a different answer. Perhaps the only truthful answer is, I am both."<br/><br/>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg' width='405' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>In <i>Epilogue</i>, Caleb is telling the story of what occured after <i>Seduced in the Dark</i> ended. I was able to get right into the swing of things without h</span>
  <span id="freeText10637983867368688285" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405576i/790308._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>♥♥♥ 5 STARS ♥♥♥</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408006i/797686._SY540_.jpg" height="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I LOVED IT!!</b> I am so glad we got to see Caleb's side!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"Who am I?<br>Am I Caleb?<br>Am I James?<br>I've often asked myself this very thing and have always come up with a different answer. Perhaps the only truthful answer is, I am both."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In <i>Epilogue</i>, Caleb is telling the story of what occured after <i>Seduced in the Dark</i> ended. I was able to get right into the swing of things without having to re-read the previous book. I loved every moment of it. The way Caleb was speaking to you as you were reading made it that much more engaging for me. I loved his sense of humor, I didn't think he could be that funny. It was enjoyable to read, as well as the banter between Caleb and Livvie. It had me smiling and chuckling.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"Everything is in the process of becoming something else. It's the law of change. I'm in the process of becoming something else, Livvie. I hope it's something good, something far removed from the monster you knew."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>This book was about them trying to get over the dark horrible past that they had experienced and hopefully move on to a brighter future. We read what Livvie's experience into Caleb's world was like, now, we are seeing how it is for Caleb to live in her world. And it was difficult for him to adjust. Being able to see inside Caleb's head, had me feeling more connected with him. I understood him a little better and his actions. I enjoyed seeing his vulnerable side as well as his sexy charming side. I fell a little more for him.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408006i/797687._SY540_.jpg" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Caleb is trying his best to improve and please Livvie. To become what she needs and can accept, by trying to hold back what is natural to him. That fact that he wanted to change for the better, was awesome to see. But he is insecure that he is not good enough for her. He also believes he may have damaged her completely. He doesn't think she will ever be able to forgive him for the way he wronged her. He is also very selfish and doesn't want to give her up.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“I wasn't sure if the Livvie I had come to know was honestly the Livvie she had been. Perhaps I had simply altered her to suit me.”<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408006i/797688._SY540_.jpg" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“I know it’s odd between us. How could it not be? We don’t know each other in this world, but I’ve seen you at your worst, and what I know is that you’d do anything to protect me. That’s enough for now. The rest will come.”<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>We get to see how they slowly try to figure out to move on from the painful memories. They know they want to be together but Livvie wants to understand how they got there. I was asking that same question. I didn't get how she could fall for her abuser, yet I was falling for him just as she was. They wanted to know what they were feeling was real, that they could trust, and get to know each other as the people they were and are now. They were on journey to finding their happiness together, one that they wanted to last, especially when they were so flawed. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408006i/797689._SY540_.jpg" height="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“No, Kitten. I’m not okay,” I whispered. “I don’t know how long it’s going to take for me to be okay. I just know that as long as you’re with me, there’s a chance that one day....I might be.”<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I loved seeing how much they both had changed and how much they have grown. It was great to see them not give up and try to heal. I loved that they were able to have a HEA. It may not be the traditional HEA, but it was one that was perfect for them. I fell in love with these characters more after reading this book. I feel as though I have come a far way, along with them through these books. I am going to really miss them now that it is over. But hopefully, we will get some short novellas? I just really don't want it to end. *sniff sniff*<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408006i/797690.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“It wasn't until Livvie walked away and I was truly alone in the world that I began to feel what love could be. It didn't come to me as it came to others; I had to find love as I had found everything else that defined me: through my suffering."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>If you loved this The Dark Duet books, I HIGHLY suggest you read this one too. It will not disappoint. Caleb's POV was done perfectly. It was a wonderful finish for a pair of deeply scarred characters. I LOVED it! This series will remain as one of my all time favorites. So give this a try.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="10637983867368688285" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('zgNfozgrgCVv5cQhG1hsmfelmH7kCE4PXfbHYSw0vZKwaUqzUgcNYMt8TEsd+lbyGieGzCCopoX7fUSYpU6jSg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('FnAmeU72CaHUYUGiy/Fx+v5Xdu81CO2sXixS1Y5n3WJoGjNpJNqE5HD4ycjNU0uRE9VoXfGoBSb4p9EsBx3Dug==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer17238056801906881825">CJ Roberts is an independent writer. She favors dark and erotic stories with taboo twists. Her work has been called sexy and disturbing in the same sentence.<br/> <br/>Her debut novel, CAPTIVE IN THE DARK, has sold over 150,000 copies and is the first of three books in her bestselling and award winning series DARK DUET.<br/><br/>She was born and raised in Southern California. Following high school, she joined the U.S</span>
  <span id="freeText17238056801906881825" style="display:none">CJ Roberts is an independent writer. She favors dark and erotic stories with taboo twists. Her work has been called sexy and disturbing in the same sentence.<br /> <br />Her debut novel, CAPTIVE IN THE DARK, has sold over 150,000 copies and is the first of three books in her bestselling and award winning series DARK DUET.<br /><br />She was born and raised in Southern California. Following high school, she joined the U.S. Air Force in 1998, served ten years and traveled the world. <br /><br />She writes short stories under the name Jennifer Roberts (<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5082404.Jennifer_Roberts">http://www.goodreads.com/author/show/...</a>)<br /><br />For more information, please visit the following:<br />Website: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://aboutcjroberts.com/index.php/books.html">http://aboutcjroberts.com/index.php/b...</a><br />Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/AuthorCJRoberts">http://www.facebook.com/AuthorCJRoberts</a><br />Twitter: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/#!/AuthorCJRoberts">https://twitter.com/#!/AuthorCJRoberts</a> </span>
